<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">hump</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">*hump</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hill, heap, thick piece</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*humpaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hip, height</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kumb-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">curved</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***homunculus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:homunculus.html>homunculus</a> (54283)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:homunculus.html>homunculus</a></i>, diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">homō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:homunculus.html>homunculus</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">homunculi</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A miniature <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>, once imagined by spermists to be present in human sperm.</li>
<li>The nerve map of the human body that exists on the parietal lobe of the human brain.</li></ol>

***hond.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hond.html>hond</a> (544)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hont</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hunt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hundaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱwn̥tós</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱwṓ</i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hund</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hound</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hond.html>hond</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:honden.html>honden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hondje.html>hondje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>dog, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:canis.html>Canis</a> lupus familiaris</i></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hont</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hunt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hundą</i>. Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:honderd.html>honderd</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hond.html>hond</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:honden.html>honden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hondje.html>hondje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> an old unit of area measuring 100 <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roeden.html>roeden</a></i>, approximately 0.14 <a href = vnd.unilang:hectares.html>hectares</a></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hondenweer.html>hondenweer</a> (75364)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hond.html>hond</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dog</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">weather</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:temps.html>temps</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:chien.html>chien</a></i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:honds.html>honds</a> (60683)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hontsch</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hond.html>hond</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dog, hound</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">denominative adjectival suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:honds.html>honds</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:honds.html>hondser</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:honds.html>honds</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">hondst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></i>) canine, relating to dogs</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (<i>concerning humans</i>) currish, doggish, doggy, notably:
<ol><li>insolent, impertinent, shameless</li>
<li>rude, coarse, insulting</li></ol></li></ol>

***hongerig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hongerig.html>hongerig</a> (6476)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hongerich</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hungragaz</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hungrugaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hungry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:honger.html>honger</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">hungrig</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hungry</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hongerig.html>hongerig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hongerig.html>hongeriger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">hongerigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hungry</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The normal Dutch expression for “I'm hungry” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:honger.html>honger</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span>literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I have hunger</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> rather than the literal equivalent <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a></i> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a></i> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hongerig.html>hongerig</a></i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> very uncommon.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">hongerigheid</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hongerig.html>hongerig</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:grote.html>grote</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:behoefte.html>behoefte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voedsel.html>voedsel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebbend.html>hebbend</a></li></ol>

***honing.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:honing.html>honing</a> (6061)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">honinch</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">honey</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:honing.html>honing</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hunangą</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">honey</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:honig.html>Honig</a></i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:honk.html>honk</a> (8693)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">honc</i>, likely through Old Dutch from Proto-Germanic *hank-, *hunk-. Only <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> cognates in the Frisian languages. Possibly related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haak.html>haak</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hook</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoek.html>hoek</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">corner</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***honkbal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:honkbal.html>honkbal</a> (4532)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:honk.html>honk</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bal.html>bal</a></i>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">baseball</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:honkbal.html>honkbal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>baseball (sport) <span class="defdate">[from ca. 1900]</span>
<ul><li><b>2009</b>, Wilna Groenenboom, <i>Document Bonaire</i>, page 91.

***hoo-ha.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoo-ha.html>hoo-ha</a> (51694)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">הו־האַ</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hu-ha</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a hullabaloo</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoo-ha.html>hoo-ha</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hoo-has</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A fuss, uproar, commotion or stir; hype; brouhaha, hullabaloo.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">There <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a big <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoo-ha.html>hoo-ha</a></b> about it in the papers, and then the world completely <a href = vnd.unilang:forgot.html>forgot</a> the matter.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> euphemistic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:vagina.html>Vagina</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vulva.html>vulva</a>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2009</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:linda.html>Linda</a> Howard,  <cite>Burn: A Novel</cite>, page 242:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>Did</a> that make her a good judge of character, or a fool who <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> letting her <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoo-ha.html>hoo-ha</a></b> do her thinking for her?</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2009</b>,  Lexi Ryan,  <cite>Stilettos, Inc.</cite>, page 163:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">She didn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> want to lose their childish battle of wills, but neither <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> she want some parasite swimming up her <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoo-ha.html>hoo-ha</a></b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2010</b>,  Dee Tenorio,  <cite>All Or Nothing</cite>, page 54:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">His mother <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> expressed disappointment that she'd <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> wrong, but by then, Belinda <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> a butterfly on her <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoo-ha.html>hoo-ha</a></b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***hoodoo.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoodoo.html>hoodoo</a> (45362)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Apparently an alteration of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:voodoo.html>voodoo</a></i>.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/%C4%90avolja_Varo%C5%A1.jpg/220px-%C4%90avolja_Varo%C5%A1.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/%C4%90avolja_Varo%C5%A1.jpg/330px-%C4%90avolja_Varo%C5%A1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/%C4%90avolja_Varo%C5%A1.jpg/440px-%C4%90avolja_Varo%C5%A1.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="800" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>Some hoodoos (spires of rock).</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/47/Tent_rocks_between_Cavusin_and_Avanos.jpg/220px-Tent_rocks_between_Cavusin_and_Avanos.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/47/Tent_rocks_between_Cavusin_and_Avanos.jpg/330px-Tent_rocks_between_Cavusin_and_Avanos.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/47/Tent_rocks_between_Cavusin_and_Avanos.jpg/440px-Tent_rocks_between_Cavusin_and_Avanos.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4272" data-file-height="2848" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>A <a href = vnd.unilang:hoodoo.html>hoodoo</a>, showing why it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also called a <a href = vnd.unilang:tent.html>tent</a> rock.</div></div></div>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoodoo.html>hoodoo</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hoodoos</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A practitioner of <a href = vnd.unilang:voodoo.html>voodoo</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Supernatural bad luck, or something or someone believed to bring bad luck.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A tall thin spire of rock that protrudes from the bottom of arid basins and <a href = vnd.unilang:badlands.html>badlands</a>.
<ul><li><b>2013</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Philipp_Meyer" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Philipp Meyer">Philipp Meyer</a>, <i>The Son</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:simon.html>Simon</a> amp; Schuster 2014, p. 71:
<dl><dd>It <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> larger than the mirage made it look—a dozen <a href = vnd.unilang:miles.html>miles</a> across and a thousand <a href = vnd.unilang:feet.html>feet</a> deep, with <a href = vnd.unilang:fins.html>fins</a> and towers and <b>hoodoos</b> like observation <a href = vnd.unilang:posts.html>posts</a>, mesas and minor buttes, springs flowing brightly in the red rock.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">spire of rock</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tent.html>tent</a> rock</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">fairy chimney</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">earth pyramid</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoodoo.html>hoodoo</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">hoodoos</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hoodooing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hoodooed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To <a href = vnd.unilang:jinx.html>jinx</a>; to bring bad luck or misfortune to.</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hôvet</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hôoft</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hōvit</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*haubudą</i>. The sense “oral sex” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Semantic_loan" class="extiw" title="w:Semantic loan">semantic loan</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">head</i>.

<ol><li>head</li>
<li>head (of an organisation), chief, boss</li>
<li>a breakwater, jetty or <a href = vnd.unilang:pier.html>pier</a> at the entrance of a sea harbour</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncommon<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> oral sex</li></ol>

***hoofddeksel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoofddeksel.html>hoofddeksel</a> (51691)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoofd.html>hoofd</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">head</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deksel.html>deksel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cover</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dekken.html>dekken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cover</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-sel</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">diminutive suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>)
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoofddeksel.html>hoofddeksel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoofddeksel.html>hoofddeksels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoofddeksel.html>hoofddekseltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A headgear, object worn as headdress</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoofdfiguur.html>hoofdfiguur</a> (69596)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoofd.html>hoofd</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">head</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:figuur.html>figuur</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">character, figure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***hoog.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoog.html>hoog</a> (1127)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hooch.html>hooch</a></i>, the original inflected <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hō-</i> reanalysed by analogy with the uninflected form because of word-final devoicing. From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hōh</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hauhaz</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">hoch</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">heech</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq"><a href = vnd.unilang:hag.html>hag</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">high</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">høj</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoog.html>hoog</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoger.html>hoger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoogst.html>hoogst</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>high
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> 887 <a href = vnd.unilang:meter.html>meter</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoge.html>hoge</a></b> <i>Mount Scenery</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoogste.html>hoogste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:punt.html>punt</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koninkrijk.html>Koninkrijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> Nederlanden.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The 887-metres-<b>high</b>  Mount Scenery <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the highest place in the Kingdom of the Netherlands.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zou.html>zou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoog.html>hoog</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gegrepen.html>gegrepen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drie.html>drie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:talen.html>talen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegelijkertijd.html>tegelijkertijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leren.html>leren</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Learning three languages simultaneously would be aiming too <b>high</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***hooggebergte.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hooggebergte.html>hooggebergte</a> (105309)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoog.html>hoog</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">high</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebergte.html>gebergte</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mountain range</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cf. <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hochgebirge</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">heechberchtme</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hooggebergte.html>hooggebergte</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hooggebergte.html>hooggebergten</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">hooggebergtes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mountain range consisting of relatively uneroded high mountains, like alps <span class="defdate">[from 18th c.]</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hauhiþō</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoog.html>hoog</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-te</i>. ***hooiwagen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hooiwagen.html>hooiwagen</a> (116729)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hooiwagen.html>hooiwagen</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hooi.html>hooi</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hay</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wagen.html>wagen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cart, wagon</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hooiwagen.html>hooiwagen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hooiwagens.html>hooiwagens</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hooiwagen.html>hooiwagentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A harvestman, an arachnid of the order Opiliones.</li>
<li>A hay cart, a wagon full of hay.</li></ol>
